Range: 0
Duration: 1 rounds/5 levels
Casting Time: 1
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None 

When this power is called upon by the Bhaalspawn, <PRO_HESHE> immediately does extra damage with each hit to <PRO_HISHER> target with any melee weapon <PRO_HESHE> wishes, whether it be fist or sword. <PRO_HISHER> dark energies travel through <PRO_HISHER> weapon to assault <PRO_HISHER> victim, allowing <PRO_HIMHER> to absorb that damage as healing to <PRO_HIMHER>self.

The effects vary by level as follows:
  10th – 14th: 2 rounds, 4 extra damage, 4 HP healed
  15th – 19th: 3 rounds, 6 extra damage, 6 HP healed

當巴爾後裔呼喚這項力量，他們瞬間可以獲得近戰武器的額外傷害（無論是拳或是劍），他們的黑暗能量會在他們的武器之中流動並且攻擊觸碰到的人，更會將傷害吸收來治療自己

@72867  = ~Found within a long-forgotten pocket of our collected pantology, herein tales the lie of the Metal "Unit." 

Gargantua was self-proclaimed lord of his immeasurable lower regions until his son, Pantagruel, questioned the accuracy of the ruler. With his shortcomings exposed, great Gargantua lay prostrate upon the ground while Pantagruel sought to cover his cuirass in case his now governing body lost its sway. He was warned that the people would cut him no slacks, but he never listened, and had burned his britches behind him. Undaunted, he fulfilled his animus with the robes of his father, as uncomfortable as that might sound, and shaped the Metal "Unit" with his own hands. 

The rule of Pantagruel was a discommoding morass, his armor eventually suffering a breach in the breech that proved his undoing. As his basket left the pantry, so to speak, his regime fell to insurrection, and so complete was the sacking that not even his Metal "Unit" could be found. The component pieces, a pantaloon triumvirate, were lost in the annals of time. 

You now bear the awesome responsibility of the Metal "Unit." Gussets of wind, seams like reality, pockets of resistance, the seat of power, and legs as flared as your temper. Polish it well; the onus is now on you.

 15 Strength

高甘塔過去在他深不可測的下層區域中自立為王，直到他兒子潘塔辜羅質疑這統治者的正當性。隨著這弱點被揭露出來，偉大的高甘塔仆街，而潘塔辜羅試圖保護自己，以防他現在的政權失去影響力。有人警告他說人們也許不會給他時間，但他從來不聽，而且還把他的長褲燒掉（破釜沉舟之意）。毫不畏懼地，他（儘管這多麼令人不快）又惡意奪取了他父親的長袍，用自己的雙手塑造出這套金屬「戰鬥裝」。

潘塔辜羅的統治紛亂無章，他的護甲最後終於在褲管的地方出現裂縫，正足以證明了他的敗亡。就好像魚離開了水，太陽離開了天空，他的政權也隨著暴亂而瓦解，那崩潰如此的混亂以至於這金屬「戰鬥裝」下落不明。這護甲的三個部分，也就是史上三大泡褲，便失落在時代的變遷中。

你現在挑起了這金屬戰鬥裝的重大責任。輕柔的褲管，如夢似幻的流線造型，可以抵擋外力的口袋，具有威力的臀部剪裁，以及那閃耀動人的大腿部分。好好地擦拭它，重擔現在落在你身上。

@73256  = ~Chapter 8

It has begun.

Even before I left Suldanessellar, the news had already begun pouring in from everywhere... tales of armies on the move, whole towns being destroyed to get at some lone wizard, massive carnage and destruction along the entire Sword Coast. It all links to the Bhaalspawn. They are being hunted, or hunting each other... whatever the case, wherever a child of Bhaal is, violence soon follows. And so the fear and panic have spread, with any innocent even suspected of having the taint being driven from their homes or killed outright.

Even the elven lands are not immune, and I sensed considerable relief upon my departure from the very city that I helped save. Ellesime, at least, offered me some advice... there is a part of the old elven woods that houses old ancestor spirits of the elves, spirits locked within giant carved faces made so long ago not even the elves remember when they were created. It is a sacred place reserved only for royalty, but Ellesime is allowing me to enter the dale and glean what wisdom I can.

I have gone alone... none of the elven forest folk want to be near me. And while no others are supposed to be here, I am sure that danger stalks me yet. I should prepare my weapons and equipment and be ready for anything...《第八章

開始了。

在我離開索丹尼斯拉之前，消息就已開始四處流傳……聽說軍隊開始行動，為了搜捕一些獨行的巫師就將數個城鎮夷為平地，整個劍灣到處都是大規模的屠殺和毀滅。一切都與巴爾後裔相關。他們被追殺，或者互相殘殺……不管什麼情況，巴爾之子所到之處，暴力立刻隨之而來。於是恐懼和驚慌蔓延開來，甚至任何無辜者只要被懷疑擁有這污穢血緣，就會被趕出家園，甚至當場被殺。

即使連精靈國度也未能免俗，因為這個曾經被我解救的城市，現在卻對我將離去而如釋重負。不過不管怎樣，艾麗星還是給了我一些建議……有一處古老的精靈族森林裡，遠古精靈祖先的靈魂被鎖在巨大的石雕頭像中，而頭像的年代卻久遠到甚至連精靈們也不記得它們是何時被創造出來的。那是精靈王族專用的聖地，但艾麗星允許我進入谷中，看看能不能獲得什麼啟示。

我得獨自前往……因為森林裡的精靈沒有一個願意靠近我。即使這裡應該四下無人，但是我敢確定有危險開始向我悄悄襲來。我該準備好武器和裝備，以面對任何將發生的事情……》~
@73257  = ~Chapter 10

All has finally been revealed to me.

Bhaal is not returning. Perhaps he might have, if evil could be counted on to do as it is asked. Bhaal left the key to his resurrection with his high priestess, and she has betrayed him, using all the power of the collected souls of Bhaal's dead children to turn herself into a goddess and leave Bhaal dead where he belongs.

Melissan tricked her former master, and she tricked me. She manipulated all the Bhaalspawn, even the members of the Five that she had collected secretly to kill the others. Even Balthazar, who didn't trust her and intended to kill her.

I am the last of Bhaal's children... but even now Melissan holds most of the power that he once had. She is in the Abyss... and my only means of getting there was to destroy the pocket plane that I had unintentionally created. I am ready to face her now.

There is no turning back.《第十章

我終於知道了一切。

巴爾沒有復活。或許他本來可以，如果能指望惡人履行諾言的話。巴爾將其復活的關鍵留給了他的高階女牧師，而她背叛了他，利用所有收集到死去巴爾之子靈魂的力量來讓她自己變成一個女神，而拋下巴爾死在他該在的地方。

梅麗珊欺騙了她的前主人，而且也欺騙了我。她操縱了所有的巴爾後裔，甚至包括她秘密召集來殺掉其餘後裔的五裔成員。甚至不信任她而且想要殺了她的巴薩扎也是。

我是最後的巴爾之子……但即使現在梅麗珊已經掌握大部分巴爾曾經擁有的力量。她在無底深淵裡……而我唯一前往的方法就是破壞掉我無意中創造的口袋空間。我現在已準備好面對她了。

不能回頭了。》~
@73258  = ~Chapter 9

Saradush has been sacked. Yaga-Shura had burst through the wall to find a Bhaalspawn... myself. I was not there, however, so he contented himself with destroying everything in his path, including all the other children of Bhaal that had sought refuge there.

Melissan survived, though she seemed devastated. I am one of the few Bhaalspawn that remain... the only others are a group comprised individually of the most powerful of Bhaal's children that remain in Faerûn. They have been hunting their siblings, including me, but to what end even Melissan doesn't know. Perhaps they seek to raise Bhaal and become his earthbound avatars. Perhaps they seek to become gods themselves. But they will not rest until I am dead... and their powers combined are enough to destroy even me, so Melissan claims.

I have little choice but to take Melissan's offer of help. She knows of a safe haven in the Calishite desert... a place called Amkethran... from which I can plan how best to confront these Bhaalspawn who hunt me and end all questions about my future and my destiny... whatever it may truly be... once and for all.《第九章

薩拉督許被攻陷了。雅加蘇拉破牆而入只為了尋找一個巴爾後裔……我。然而我並不在那兒，於是他只能一路摧毀所見之物，包括所有其他在那兒避難的巴爾之子。

梅麗珊倖存下來，雖然她似乎身心俱疲。我是殘留的少數巴爾後裔之一……其餘僅有的幾個是費倫剩下的最強的巴爾之子群組成的一群。他們追殺他們的手足，包括我，但是為了什麼甚至連梅麗珊也不知道。或許他們想要讓巴爾復活並成為他凡間的化身。或許他們試圖讓自己成為神。但他們不會停止，直到我死亡……如梅麗珊所宣稱，他們聯合的力量甚至足夠摧毀我。

我沒有什麼選擇只能接受梅麗珊提供的幫助。她知道在卡林沙漠有一個安全的避難所……一個叫安姆克薩藍的地方……在那裡我可以計劃一下如何好好迎擊這些追殺我的巴爾後裔，並結束所有關於我的未來和命運的問題……不管它真正是什麼……完完全全地結束。》~

@73864  = ~Revelations of the Solar

The powerful Bhaalspawn that I have been fighting, the ones that have been relentlessly hunting the others, call themselves "the Five." Like myself, they are the most potent of our kind and possess a great deal of Bhaal's divine essence.

It appears that they had gathered together for a single purpose... since they were too powerful to fight each other, they would combine their forces and hunt the remainder of the Bhaalspawn. Then they would raise our sire and become his earthly generals. They were largely successful, but four of them are now dead: Illasera, Yaga-Shura, Sendai, and Abazigal.

The only trick is that they contained so much of Bhaal's essence that the god may be nearer to resurrection than ever. Perhaps that is what the last of the Five, Balthazar, plans even now. I have no choice but to return to Amkethran and stop him. Then, perhaps, this will finally all be over.

For all her risks, Mazzy eventually passed peacefully at a ripe old age, knowing she could take pride in everything she had done.《瑪茲·芬頓和<CHARNAME>一起面對的危險並沒有阻止她對於冒險的渴望。事實上，在泰斯爾的事件結束後不久她就群組建了芬頓騎士團，一支在國度上創造了許多英勇事績的堅毅隊伍。他們和巨魔戰鬥並拯救了陷入危險的城鎮，擊退潮水般的獸人以保護古老的森林，在一隻惡龍的巢穴面對它只為了使世界更安全。他們的傳奇比生命更有意義，對瑪茲而言更是如此。有人說如果勇氣可以用尺寸來丈量的話，那麼她就有二十尺高。儘管經歷過種種危險，直到晚年瑪茲仍安然無恙，她知道她可以為她做過的每件事情都感到驕傲自豪。》~
@73933  = ~Jan Jansen's life following his association with <CHARNAME> was typically convoluted, the barest of details hidden amidst his half-truths and whole lies. According to his published memoirs, "A Jansen in Every Port," after a short prison term for monkey smuggling, he returned to his first love... monkey smuggling. This led to the now infamous Gibbon Riot of '72, a tumultuous and altogether unclean event that seemed to center on the estate of the Shadow Thief Vaelag. Jan would deny that he had planned the downfall of the rogue, but he was unable to explain what practical application he had intended for a horde of knife-wielding simians. Nevertheless, the death of the admittedly disliked and generally suspect Vaelag could not be attributed to the young gnome. Strangely enough, Jan had alibis for each and every second of the day in question, and what a day it must have been! Relatives from across the realms came forward to say that he had stopped in for tea and turnips. At his later wedding to Lissa, Jan was asked how he managed to be in so many places at once and yet still so far from the scene of the crime. "Well," Jan would say, "when you have that many monkeys, anything is possible."《在結束與<CHARNAME>的合作之後，姚恩·姚森的生活極為曲折離奇，僅有的一點細節隱藏在他那半真半假或者乾脆都是騙人的謊言之中。根據他出版的回憶錄「姚森在每個港口」介紹，在因走私猴子而被短暫囚禁後，他重回他的最愛……走私猴子。這導致了目前臭名昭著的72長臂猿暴動事件，這起騷亂或者說陰謀似乎與影賊維拉格的宅邸有關。姚恩否認他策劃了對那個流氓的謀殺，但是他無法解釋他打算拿一群揮舞刀子的類人猿作什麼實際應用。儘管如此，被公認為不受歡迎而且可疑的維拉格的死無法歸咎於這位年輕的侏儒。奇怪的是，姚恩對於案發的那一天有完全的不在場證明，那是什麼樣的一天啊！姚恩在被遺忘的國度上的所有親戚都出面說那天他曾為了茶和蕪菁而在他們那裡稍作停留。之後在他與麗莎的婚禮上，姚恩被問到他如何能夠同時出現在那麼多地方，卻又遠離犯罪現場。「好吧，」姚恩會回答，「當你有這麼多猴子時，什麼事都是可能的。」》~

@73945  = ~Elminster's Ecologies: Appendix IIIa《伊爾明斯特生態學：附錄IIIa》~
@73946  = ~Elminster's Ecologies: Appendix IIIa

This timeworn tome is written by the sage Elminster and apparently part of a much larger body of work containing detailed studies of most of the strange creatures from around Faerûn. 

The appendix seems to refer to newly discovered variations on normal breeds of creatures. Of particular interest:

"Dense Puddings—a relative of the slimes and molds, this pudding is relatively normal... except when exposed to electricity or fire. When this occurs, it splits into new puddings and can therefore be very dangerous."

"Fire Trolls—a new form of troll thought to have been created by sorcerous fire giants for use as servants and guards. They are similar to regular trolls in most respects except for their lava-temperature skin and burning touch. Once they are defeated, they can only be permanently killed by cold or acid."

"Fission Slime—an offshoot of the slimes and molds, this particular slime will split into new and independent creatures when hit. It is vulnerable to fire, which will kill it permanently."

"Magic Golems—this rare type of golem is formed from pure magical energy and is completely immune to spellcraft as well as enchanted weapons. To my knowledge, only weapons without enchantments have any effects on this creature."

"Mariliths—while this is apparently a legitimate form of demon, it is one that only an exceptional few have encountered and survived. The marilith is a six-armed demon with a human female front half and the back half of a snake. She is incredibly quick and deadly, and on top of her martial prowess with six swords, she casts spells as well. Fighters should beware: In addition to being immune to normal weapons and minor enchantments, this demon also likes to cast protection from magical weapons... which must be dispelled if a fighter is to have any chance with his armaments."《伊爾明斯特生態學：附錄IIIa

這陳舊的書卷是由聖者伊爾明斯特所著，而且明顯地是一大得多、包含費倫各地許多奇怪生物詳細研究的工作內容的一部分。

這附錄似乎是與生物正常品種新發現的變異種有關。特別有趣的是：

「濃稠布丁怪－－黏液及黏怪的親戚，這種布丁怪相對來說較正常……除非暴露於電或火的時候。當這種情形發生時它會分裂出新的布丁怪而因此會很危險。」

「火巨魔－－一種新型的巨魔被認為是由火巨人法師創造來當僕人及守衛。在大部分方面他們和普通巨魔一樣除了溫度和熔岩一樣的皮膚及灼熱的碰觸。他們一但被擊倒，只有冷或酸能永遠殺死他們。」

「融合黏液－－黏液及黏怪的旁支，這種特別的黏液被擊中時會分裂成新的獨立生物。它易被火傷害，這可以永遠殺死它」

「魔法巨像－－這種稀有的魔像是由純粹的魔法能量所形成且對法術以及魔法武器完全免疫。就我所知，只有沒有魔法加持的武器才對這種生物有效。」

「六臂蛇魔－－這明顯的是一種正統的惡魔，只有少數人能夠在遭遇她們之後還能存活下來。六臂蛇魔是有六隻手臂的惡魔而且有人類女性的前面半身及蛇的背部。她快的驚人並且致命，除了她手持六把劍武威善戰之外，她也能施法。戰士必須注意：除了對普通武器及次等魔法武器免疫之外，這惡魔也喜歡施展魔法武器免疫術……假如戰士有任何機會使用裝備的話必須先破解它。」》~

職業優勢：

–第2級：每天可施放一次日魂射線
	日魂射線：日魂武僧從<PRO_HISHER>張開的手掌射出一道強光，每2等級造成1d8火焰傷害，最大值為5d8，對不死生物額外造成6點傷害。
–第5級：每天可施放一次燃燒之拳
	燃燒之拳：日魂武僧將體內的光明之力導向徒手攻擊，令雙拳變為可在下一輪造成2d6額外火焰傷害的燃燒武器。效果持續時間將在等級9時增加至2輪，在等級12時增加至3輪，在等級15時增加至4輪，在等級25時增加至5輪。該特殊能力自動修正普通攻擊，無需切換武器。
–第6級：日魂射線的使用次數增加1次
–第8級：每天可施放一次聖日術
	聖日術：日魂武僧將自己籠罩在一層火焰之中，效果如同火焰護盾（紅），為武僧增加50%火焰抗性，同時可防護來自半徑5呎內的攻擊。在該距離內通過任何武器或法術攻擊武僧的對手都會受到1d8+2火焰傷害。
–第10級：日魂射線的使用次數增加1次
–第13級：每天可施放一次日魂光束
	日魂光束：日魂武僧射出一道耀眼的光芒，可擊中半徑30呎內的其他生物。日魂光束並不會自動擊中全部目標，而是根據武僧當前的零級命中值（對不死生物額外+3）對範圍內生物進行一次近戰攻擊。被擊中的生物會受到9d6傷害（不死生物受到9d6+3傷害），通過對法術的豁免檢定可將傷害減半。此外，範圍內除武僧之外的生物都需要通過對法術的豁免檢定，否則會失明2小時。
–第15級：日魂射線的使用次數增加1次

職業限制：

–陣營限制為守序善良
–無法使用震眩拳能力
–無法使用穿震掌能力》~

@77512  = ~blackguard《黑衛》~
@77513  = ~Blackguard《黑衛》~
@77514  = ~BLACKGUARD: The Blackguard epitomizes evil and is nothing short of a mortal fiend. The quintessential black knight, this villain carries a reputation of the foulest sort that is very well deserved. Consorting with demons and devils and serving dark deities, the Blackguard is hated and feared by all. Some people call these villains "anti-paladins" due to their completely evil nature.

Advantages:
– Immune to level drain and fear.
– May turn undead as a Paladin of the same level.
– May use the Absorb Health ability once per day.

ABSORB HEALTH:
Deals 2 points of damage per level to an enemy, healing the Blackguard the same number of Hit Points.

– May use the Poison Weapon ability once per day. Gains one use at level 1, one use at level 5, and an additional use every 5 levels thereafter.

Poison Weapon
Each successful hit within the next 5 rounds will inject poison into the target. Each target can only be affected once per round. The amount of poison damage depends on the character's level:

1st - Target suffers 1 poison damage per second for 6 seconds (Save vs. Death at +1 negates)
5th - Target suffers 1 poison damage per second for 12 seconds (Save vs. Death negates), and also immediately suffers 2 poison damage (no save)
9th - Target suffers 1 poison damage per second for 18 seconds (Save vs. Death at -1 negates), and also immediately suffers 4 poison damage (no save)
13th - Target suffers 1 poison damage per second for 24 seconds (Save vs. Death at -2 negates), and also immediately suffers 6 poison damage (no save)

– 3rd level: May use the Aura of Despair ability once per day.

AURA OF DESPAIR: When this ability is activated, all enemies within 15 feet of the Blackguard suffer ill effects based on the Blackguard's level:
  3rd level - All enemies suffer a -1 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -2 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn.
  6th level - All enemies suffer a -2 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -2 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn.
  15th level - All enemies suffer a -4 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -4 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn; enemies with 8 or fewer Hit Dice are panicked as well.
  20th Level - All enemies suffer a -4 penalty to hit and damage rolls and a -4 penalty to Armor Class for 1 turn; enemies with 18 or fewer Hit Dice are panicked as well.

Disadvantages:
– Alignment restricted to evil.
– May not cast Detect Evil.
– May not cast Protection From Evil as an innate ability.
– May not use the Lay on Hands ability.《黑衛是邪惡的象徵，完全可以說他們是凡人之軀的魔王。作為典型的黑色騎士，這些惡徒帶著理所當然的污穢名聲。他們與惡魔和魔鬼同行，並服務於黑暗神祇，黑衛被所有人憎恨和恐懼。出於他們完全邪惡的本質，有些人稱這些惡徒為「反聖武士」。

職業優勢：
–免疫等級吸取和恐懼
–能夠像同等級的聖武士一樣超渡不死生物
–每天能夠使用一次吸取生命能力
	吸取生命：對一個敵人造成每等級2點傷害，治療施法者相同數值的生命值。
–每提升5個等級，每天就可以多使用1次淬毒武器能力（等級為1時每天可使用1次）
	淬毒武器：在5輪時間內，每次成功命中都能將毒液灌入目標體內。目標每輪只會受到一次毒液的影響，角色的等級決定具體傷害：
	1級：目標每秒收到1點毒素傷害，持續6秒（以+1有利通過對死亡的豁免檢定則可避免中毒）
	5級：目標立刻收到2點毒素傷害（無豁免），之後每秒收到1點毒素傷害，持續12秒（通過對死亡的豁免檢定則可避免中毒）
	9級：目標立刻收到4點毒素傷害（無豁免），之後每秒收到1點毒素傷害，持續18秒（以-1不利通過對死亡的豁免檢定則可避免中毒）
	13級：目標立刻收到6點毒素傷害（無豁免），之後每秒收到1點毒素傷害，持續24秒（以-1不利通過對死亡的豁免檢定則可避免中毒）
–每天能夠使用一次絕望光環能力（始於第3級），效果隨等級提升增強，30呎內的敵人都將受到以下效果影響，具體取決於施法者的等級（無豁免）：
	3級：命中和傷害-1不利，防禦等級-2不利，持續1回合。
	6級：命中和傷害-2不利，防禦等級-2不利，持續1回合。
	15級：命中和傷害-4不利，防禦等級-4不利，持續1回合；對於等級8及以下的敵人造成恐懼效果。
	20級：命中和傷害-4不利，防禦等級-4不利，持續1回合；對於等級18及以下的敵人造成恐懼效果。

@80043  = ~Worshippers of Shar favor stealth, secrecy, and the cover of darkness. These boots are tailor-made for that mindset, and are obviously linked to Shar in some way. The Night Walkers, as they are called, aren't made from the hide of any known beast, and appear darker than a midnight sky.

While the boots lack any sort of magical aura, they provide the wearer with several benefits. Anyone wearing the Night Walkers moves more quickly, and their movement cannot be restricted. The boots also allow the wearer to hide from sight, enabling quick escape.

STATISTICS:

Equipped abilities:
– Movement rate increased by 2 (base is 9)
– Immunity to Web, Grease, and Entangle

Charge abilities:
– Shadow Door three times per day
  Duration: 9 rounds

Weight: 3《莎爾信徒喜歡潛行、秘密行動、以及黑暗的掩護。這些靴子為此製作，顯然以某種方式與莎爾相關。它們被稱為夜行者，不是用任何已知動物的皮革製成，看上去比午夜的天空還要黑暗。

雖然靴子似乎並無任何魔法靈光，但它們給穿戴者提供了許多好處。穿上夜行者的人移動得更快，其行動不受限制。靴子還允許穿戴者躲避視線，從而快速逃脫。

資料資料：

裝備能力：
-移動速度+2（基礎10）
-免疫蛛網、油膩和糾纏

充能能力：
-每天三次暗影門
	持續時間：9輪
	
重量：3》~
